def near_fifty(n):
    return ((n >= 40) and (n <60 ) or (n >= 140) and (n < 160))

def near_fifty(n):
    return ((n>=40 and n<=60) or (n>=140 and n<=160))

def near_fifty(n):
    if (n - 50 >= -10 and n - 50 <=10) or (n - 150 >= -10 and n - 150 <=10):
        return True
    return False

def near_fifty(n):
    if (n-50>-11 and n-50<11) or (n-150>-11 and n-150<11):
        return True
    return False

def near_fifty(n):
    if (n%50>39) or (n%50<11) and (n%50>0):
        return True
    else:
        return False

def near_fifty(n):
    if 39 < n < 61 :
        return True
    if 139 < n < 161:
        return True
    else:
        return False

def near_fifty(n):
    if n<50 and n-50>=-10:
        return True
    elif n>50 and n<150 and (n-50<=10 or n-150>=-10):
        return True
    elif n>150 and n-150<=10:
        return True
    else:
        return False

def near_fifty(n):
    d = 10
    return (n>=50-d and n<=50+d)or(n>=150-d and n<=150+d)

def near_fifty(n):
    for x in 50, 150:
        if n >= x - 10 and n <= x + 10:
            return True
    return False

def near_fifty(n):
    if 39<n<61:
        return True
    elif 139<n<161:
        return True
    else:
        return False

def near_fifty(n):
    if 60>=n>=40:
        return True
    elif 160>=n>=140:
        return True
    else:
        return False
        

def near_fifty(n):
    if n>39 and n<61 or n139 and n<161:
        print("True")
    else:
        print("False")
    return print(end="")

def near_fifty(n):
    return (40<=n<=60) or (140<=n<=160)

def near_fifty(n):
    x = abs(50 - n)
    y = abs(150 - n)
    if y <= 10:
        return True
    
    if x <= 10:
        return True
    else:
        return False    
    return y or x
    

def near_fifty(n):
    if 61>n>39:
    	return True
    elif 161>n>139:
    	return True
    else: return False

def near_fifty(n):
    if (n < 50 and (50 - n <= 10)) or (n > 50 and ( n - 50 <= 10))or (n < 150 and (150 - n <= 10)) or (n > 150 and ( n - 150 <= 10)):
    	return True
    else:
        return False

def near_fifty(n):
    return 40<=n<=60 or 140<=n<=160

def near_fifty(n):
    if (40 <= n <= 60) | (140 <= n <= 160):
        return True
    else:
        return False

def near_fifty(n):
    if 40 <= n <= 50 or 140<= n <=150:
        return True
    elif 50 <= n <= 60 or 150<= n <=160:
        return True
    return False

def near_fifty(n):
    if n<161 and n>139:
        return True
    if n<61 and n39:
        return True
    else:
   		return False

def near_fifty(n):
    if  n -10 <= 50 and n +10 >= 50:
    	return True
    elif n -10 <= 150 and n +10 >= 150:
        return True
    else:	
        return False


def near_fifty(n):
    if ((n - 150) < 11 and (n - 150)  -11) or ((n - 50) < 11 and (n - 50) > -11):
        return True
    return False

def near_fifty(n):
    return (n <= 160 and n >= 140) or (n <= 60 and n >= 40)

def near_fifty(n):
    if (n in range(50-10, 50+11)) or (n in range(150-10, 150+11)):
        return True
    else:
    	return False

def near_fifty(n):
    range1 = (140,161)
    range2 = (40,61)
    if (n >= range1[0] and n < range1[1]) or (n >= range2[0] and n < range2[1]):
        return  True
    return False

def near_fifty(n):
    for i in range(11):
        if 50 + i == n or 50 - i == n or 150 + i == n or 150 - i == n:
            return True
    return False

def near_fifty(n):
    if 11 (n - 50) > -11 or 11 >(n - 150)  -11:
        return True
    
    return False

def near_fifty(n):
    i = n+10
    o = n-10
    if (i>=50 and o<=50) or (i>=150 and o<=150):
        return True
    else:
        return False

def near_fifty(n):
    if n in range(39, 61):
        return True
    elif n in range(139, 161):
        return True
    return False

def near_fifty(n):
    x = n = 40 and n <= 60
    y = n >= 140 and n <= 160
    if x or y:        
    	return True
    else:
        return False

def near_fifty(n):
    a = 0
    for i in range(40,61,1):
        if n == i:
            a += 1
            return True
    for i in range(140,161,1):
        if n == i:
            a+=1
            return True
    if a == 0:
        return False
def near_fifty(n):
    return min(abs(n - 50), abs(n - 150)) <= 10

def near_fifty(n):
    '''if ((n < 40) or ((n > 60 ) and (n < 140) or (n > 160)):'''
    if (n < 40) or ((n > 60) and (n < 140)) or (n > 160):
    	return False
    else: return True  
                  

def near_fifty(n):
    if n < 40 : return False
    if n > 160 : return False
    if n > 40 :
        if n < 60 : return True
    if n > 140 :
        if n < 160 : return True
    if n is 160 : return True
    if n is 140 : return True
    if n is 60 : return True
    if n is 40 : return True

def near_fifty(n):
    if n <= 60 and n >=40:
     	for value in range(40, 60):
     		if n == value:
     			#print(n,value)
     			return True
     		else:
     			pass
    elif n <= 160 and n >=140:
     	return True

    else:
    	return False

    if (50 - n) / 10 <= 1 and (50 - n) / 10 >= -1:
        return True
    elif (150 - n) / 10 <= 1 and (150 - n) / 10 >= -1:
        return True
    else:
        return False

    if n > 140 :
        if n < 160 : return True
    if n is 160 : return True
    if n is 140 : return True
    if n is 60 : return True
    if n is 40 : return True

def near_fifty(n):
    if n <= 60 and n >=40:
     	for value in range(40, 60):
     		if n == value:
     			#print(n,value)
     			return True
     		else:
     			pass
    elif n <= 160 and n >=140:
     	return True

    else:
    	return False

def near_fifty(n):
    a = 0
    for i in range(40,61,1):
        if n == i:
            a += 1
            return True
    for i in range(140,161,1):
        if n == i:
            a+=1
            return True
    if a == 0:
        return False

    if n is 160 : return True

    if n is 60 : return True
    if n is 40 : return True

    if n <= 60 and n >=40:
     	for value in range(40, 60):
     		if n == value:
     			#print(n,value)
     			return True
     		else:
     			pass
    elif n <= 160 and n >=140:
     	return True

    else:
    	return False

def near_fifty(n):
    a = 0
    for i in range(40,61,1):
        if n == i:
            a += 1
            return True
    for i in range(140,161,1):
        if n == i:
            a+=1
            return True
    if a == 0:
        return False

    return False

    return False

    if n is 160 : return True

    if n is 60 : return True
    if n is 40 : return True

    if n <= 60 and n >=40:
     	for value in range(40, 60):
     		if n == value:
     			#print(n,value)
     			return True
     		else:
     			pass
    elif n <= 160 and n >=140:
     	return True

    else:
    	return False

def near_fifty(n):
    a = 0
    for i in range(40,61,1):
        if n == i:
            a += 1
            return True
    for i in range(140,161,1):
        if n == i:
            a+=1
            return True
    if a == 0:
        return False

    return False

    return False
